Guangdong Province Prepares to Ban Gambling Next Year 63

Requests the Central Government to Repay Public Bonds Issued by the Former Ministry of Finance

Guangzhou Dispatch: The Department of Finance is currently preparing to ban gambling throughout the province next year in order to eliminate the long-standing gambling scourge that has plagued the people of Guangdong. It has been found that the annual gambling tax in Guangdong Province is about 10 million yuan, accounting for half of the province's annual revenue. Once this huge income is stopped, the province's budget will be severely affected. Therefore, the financial authorities are currently planning to reduce military spending, and at the same time, they are trying to investigate various tax revenues and collect special taxes to make up for the loss. On the other hand, there are still more than 20 million yuan of the first, second, and third-class public bonds issued by the former Ministry of Finance in Guangdong that have not been repaid. This money should be repaid by the Central Government. If the province implements a gambling ban next year, the provincial treasury will suffer a sudden loss and will have no surplus to repay this debt for the Ministry of Finance. Fan Caichang, Director of the Department of Finance, has already submitted this matter to the provincial government and forwarded it to the Central Government for verification. The original submission roughly stated that the Ministry of Finance is now setting up a committee to reorganize domestic and foreign debts, which will be established soon. Regarding the scope of the reorganization, it is stipulated that it is limited to the Central Government. The aforementioned public bonds were issued by the former Ministry of Finance in Guangdong, and the original plan for the financial public bonds issued in the 17th year was also for the purpose of coordinating the financial expenditure of various public bonds. It seems that it is different from the local situation of the province and should be included in the scope of the Central Government, and the entire committee should handle the cases together in order to clarify the central and local systems and clear the boundaries. It is reasonable to request your government to submit the case to the Executive Yuan and consult the Ministry of Finance, so that the Ministry can repay the debt and submit the case to the Committee for the Reorganization of Domestic and Foreign Debts to handle the cases together, etc. It is rumored that the motive for this matter stems from the fact that in September of this year, Chen Mingshu, chairman of the provincial government, proposed to the Central Political Conference that Guangdong Province plans to ban gambling this year, but the public bonds issued by the former Ministry of Finance in Guangdong have not been repaid to this day, with a principal of more than 20 million yuan, and it is proposed that the Central Government repay them, or replace the old bonds with new bonds to reduce the burden on Guangdong Province. The Central Political Conference decided to approve this and send it to Guangdong. Therefore, Director Fan Cai had this submission.

Guangzhou Permanently Stops Collecting Housing Rent 64

Already Passed by the Guangdong Provincial Government Meeting

Guangzhou Correspondence: Since the Guangdong Province began collecting housing rental surcharges, the excessive levies and disturbances have been unmatched. Several years ago, due to military relations, the government often collected three months' worth of rent out of the twelve months of the year.

Page 10

Landlords, suffering this loss, raised the original rental values to compensate for the government's borrowing. As a result, this exploitation was passed on to the property-less tenants. Recently, Guangzhou's rents have continued to rise, creating a situation where it is difficult to live in Guangzhou. Moreover, this type of surcharge not only harmed ordinary people, but also greatly affected the police expenses of public security organs. Recently, Ouyang Ju, the Director of the Public Security Bureau, based on these reasons, specially proposed to permanently stop the collection of rental surcharges and submitted a request to the provincial government for approval. His memorial stated: "Since the Republic of China's twelfth year, whenever there has been a special need or a significant deficit in the treasury, rental surcharges have been levied in this city to swiftly collect large sums of money to cope with the situation. Once this precedent was set, it became a fixed practice. In recent years, due to frequent local disturbances, the supplies needed were enormous, and the case was cited for collection. Up to now, it has been done eighteen times, totaling more than thirteen million. This corner of the urban area has an increased burden of ten million, which is truly exhausting all resources and draining the pond to catch the fish. After the chaos, amidst the ashes, households lack savings. Although Guangzhou is prosperous, it seems to have returned to its former state, but mending the house requires pulling grass, and it is no longer what it used to be. Those who make a living by collecting rent rely on monthly rent for their daily needs. After paying the police surcharge, the remaining amount is barely enough. The suffering of repeatedly being taxed is well known. In recent years, citizens, fearing the collection of rental surcharges, have assumed two months of surcharges and two months of vacancy when calculating property income, budgeting for only eight months of rent per year. Comparing today's land prices and construction costs to the principal and interest, the interest rate is very low. Existing shops have no choice but to increase rent to offset the loss, causing potential investors to hesitate and renters to frown and complain. This has negatively impacted the city's construction and prosperous development. Moreover, citizens, out of concern for rental surcharges, often underreport rental amounts for police expenses, hoping to reduce the burden. Although there are penalties for false reporting and strict inspections, they resort to risky and侥倖 strategies due to repeated levies, leading to widespread underreporting. As a result, the regular income of the bureau is greatly reduced. Also, due to the collection of police surcharges, the workload of clerks and staff has doubled, leaving them with no time to handle the police fees that should be collected. Citizens, having already paid huge rental surcharges, are unable to pay the police fees again. Although the collection is strictly enforced, it has reached its limit, and the accumulation of arrears is a major reason. If this collection of rental surcharges has no end, not only will the people's lives become increasingly difficult, but the development of the urban area will also gradually decline, and the bureau's expenses will also gradually decrease. The public and private sectors are both in difficulty, and the relationship is significant. Citizens have repeatedly requested and pleaded for a permanent cessation of the collection. The bureau director believes that the government's collection of rental surcharges was originally a last resort, as raising other funds would be too slow to be effective, so it is better to collect nearby to meet local needs. Considering the citizens' enthusiasm for public welfare, it was a temporary measure of cutting flesh to heal wounds, and there is no reason to criticize it. Recently, the government has also been deeply concerned about rental surcharges before proceeding. The original intention was not to cause suffering to the people. For example, this time, to raise funds to suppress the rebellion, one month of financial borrowing was collected, stating that it was a temporary loan, which was to alleviate the people's hardships. It has now been repaid on schedule, which is different from previous rental surcharges. The citizens, admiring the government's kindness, all hope that the collection will be permanently stopped in the future to relieve the people's suffering. Collecting three or four times a year is no different from insatiable demands, and the burden all comes from the urban area, which seems unfair. As the director of the police administration, I am close to the citizens, silently observing the current economic situation of the city and the demands of public opinion. What I have seen and heard is verifiable and I dare not suppress it from above. I offer my humble opinions, not daring to seek praise. Whether to issue a clear order to permanently stop the collection of rental surcharges in the future to show sympathy and comply with public opinion should be submitted to the higher government for review and implementation." After receiving the submission, the provincial government proposed it at the 125th provincial affairs meeting on the 5th for discussion. It was immediately resolved to issue a proclamation as requested to permanently stop the collection and ordered the Department of Finance to comply. (December 6)

Large Band of Fierce Bandits Discovered in Western Shenyang 67

Shenyang Correspondence: Shenyang County and Xinmin County are adjacent. On the night of the 3rd of this month, a large band of mounted bandits suddenly emerged from Xinmin to Panggutai in the seventh district of western Shenyang. There were about a hundred or more bandits, each equipped with a large rifle and a pistol. Among them, some even carried two pistols. The bandits had ample ammunition for both large and small guns, their horsemanship was extremely skilled, and they brought their own food. After staying for about a day, they left the area without robbing or kidnapping. It was said that their intention was solely to collect food. The local public security sub-bureau, aware of the situation, notified the general bureau by telephone because the bandits were numerous and the police were few. Zhang Detang, the director of the County Public Security Bureau, immediately led a team to rush there. By the time they reached the area, the bandits had already left. To demonstrate their strength and deter the bandits, the police team conducted artillery drills outside the village, the sound of which resonated far and wide. Seeing no trace of the bandits, they returned in formation. Unexpectedly, the bandits, after leaving the area, learned that the police team had led a group to pursue them and had conducted artillery drills to demonstrate their strength. They then returned to confront the police team and vowed to fight to the death. They also told the villagers that they had not intended to harm the villagers of the Shenyang area, but the revenge for the police team's pursuit had to be taken. They said that their departure earlier was voluntary and not because they were frightened away by the police team. After the bandits returned, they looted everywhere and kidnapped many wealthy people in the area, stationing themselves in Panggutai Village. Upon hearing the alarm, the local public security sub-bureau sent a team to engage the bandits once. Unexpectedly, the bandits were extremely fierce, and several police officers were killed in action. The sub-bureau urgently reported to the general bureau, and Director Zhang Detang again led a team to the village at night to confront the bandits. From the afternoon of the 4th to the morning of the 5th, gunshots rang out intermittently in the darkness and snow. By sunrise, most of the county's artillery and public security teams had gathered in the village, preparing to launch a general attack on the bandits. The bandits then gradually moved north, and the police team did not dare to pursue them closely, but took a gradual encirclement approach. At the same time, the Fourth and Fifth Companies of the Public Security Infantry were also mobilized to converge on the area to participate in the suppression. A team was sent to the province to request a large batch of guns and ammunition for resupply. It is said that this band of bandits is extremely barbaric and may not be eliminated within a day or two. It is also said that the bandits were originally from the military and had experienced many battles. Their current desperate act poses a significant hidden danger to the area. (December 6)

The heads of the Yanji City and County Public Security Bureaus also came to the province one after another to discuss everything. Jiangsu Province Plans to Dredge the Shallow Sections of the Li Canal 70

The Canal Works Office Has Two Proposed Plans

The Jiangbei Li Canal in Jiangsu Province, from Gaoyou to Jieshou, is the most shallow and narrow section and is prone to siltation. Every winter, when the canal water is low, the inflow from the Ziying Sluice into the lower canal is excessively strong, and the inflow of lake water into the canal from the Jiusheng Port increases, causing the section north of Mapeng Bay to often reverse flow. In the 11th and 12th years of the Republic of China (1922-1923), the former Transport Supervision Bureau used manual dredging once. Later, at the request of the Baoying people to rebuild the sluice gates to facilitate farmland irrigation, Yong'an Sluice, Zhangcheng Hole, etc., were dismantled and rebuilt, and the Jinmen was lowered and enlarged, reducing the amount of water. During periods of low water, the canal flow in this section became weaker, causing the previously dredged areas to become silted again within a few years. The storage capacity was reduced, and traffic and irrigation became difficult. In recent years, drought has been a disaster, and the people along the canal have repeatedly requested dredging. The former Canal Engineering Bureau planned to first dredge the Zhangfu Water Diversion Field to increase the upper stream water source of the canal, and then seek to regulate the ports on the west bank of the Li Canal bed to equalize the flow and reduce siltation. However, the Zhangfu River project was ordered by the Construction Committee to be included in the Huai River Diversion project and handled jointly, so it was not carried out. The former Canal Engineering Office revised its plan to first use manual dredging to dredge the shallow sections of the Li Canal near Gaobao, starting from Yangjiamiao in Huaian to Yuehe Port in Gaoyou, with all the projects being carried out simultaneously. Then, a new sluice gate would be built on the west bank of the Sishui flood section to divert water from the lake to help the canal, while deepening the Tonghu Sluice Hole diversion canal and changing the Jiusheng Port entrance to ensure that the two waters of the river and canal would flow smoothly after meeting. However, due to the large project and huge funds, it was not easy to raise funds. In addition, the original savings from the canal management land tax and other miscellaneous taxes were insufficient to cover the expenses. Therefore, the project was changed to annual and sectional dredging, first selecting the silted sections for construction and dredging, in order to improve them gradually. The former Canal Engineering Office prepared a plan to divide the dredging into four sections step by step, and the third section, which was the most silted and narrowest, from Zhangcheng Hole in Sishui to Jiusheng Port in Mapeng, with a length of twenty-five kilometers, was selected for the first dredging. All the construction surveys, engineering plans, budget charts, etc., for this section have been completed and submitted to the Water Conservancy Bureau. According to the plan, there are two options for consideration and implementation based on financial resources. The first option is to excavate the river bottom to a width of twelve meters, with a slope of two on both sides, removing more than 155,000 cubic meters of earth. The estimated cost, including the construction of dams and water pumps, is about 152,000 silver dollars. The second option is to excavate the river bottom to a width of nine meters, with a slope of two on both sides, removing more than 109,000 cubic meters of earth. The estimated cost, including the construction of dams and water pumps, is about 108,000 silver dollars. The above two options were proposed by the former Canal Engineering Office to the Council of Advisers and were approved. The second option was adopted because it was easier to implement. It is now heard that the Water Conservancy Bureau has submitted it to the Construction Department for approval and is preparing everything. The necessary funds are also being actively planned for, aiming to start construction in the winter when the water recedes and the farmers are free, and to complete all the work before the rice planting season in the spring. During the construction period, the shipping traffic in this section will be handled as usual, with the Shipping Association notifying the boat owners and small steamers to divert from the Baoying North Sluice diversion canal and the Mapeng Bay Jiusheng Port, passing through the lake and detouring.

Complete Text of the Family Section of the Civil Code (Continuation 6) 71

Chapter 5: Support (Article 1114) The following relatives have a mutual obligation to provide support: (1) Lineal relatives to each other; (2) One spouse living with the other spouse's parents, to each other; (3) Siblings to each other; (4) Head of the family and family members to each other. (Article 1115) When there are several persons obligated to provide support, the order in which they should fulfill their obligations shall be determined as follows: (1) Lineal relatives in the descending line; (2) Lineal relatives in the ascending line; (3) Head of the family; (4) Siblings; (5) Family members; (6) Sons and daughters-in-law; (7) Parents of the spouse. If there are several lineal ascendants or lineal descendants, the one with the closest degree of kinship shall have priority. If there are several persons obligated to provide support and they are of the same degree of kinship, they shall each share the obligation according to their financial capacity. (Article 1116) When there are several persons entitled to receive support, and the financial capacity of the person obligated to provide support is insufficient to support all of them, the persons to be supported shall be determined in the following order: (1) Lineal relatives in the ascending line; (2) Lineal relatives in the descending line; (3) Family members; (4) Siblings; (5) Head of the family; (6) Parents of the spouse; (7) Sons and daughters-in-law. If there are several lineal ascendants or lineal descendants, the one with the closest degree of kinship shall have priority. If there are several persons entitled to receive support and they are of the same degree of kinship, support shall be provided according to their needs. (Article 1117) The right to receive support is limited to those who cannot maintain their livelihood and have no ability to earn a living. The restriction of the inability to earn a living in the preceding paragraph does not apply to lineal ascendants. (Article 1118) A person who cannot maintain their own livelihood due to the burden of providing support is exempted from their obligation. (Article 1119) The extent of support shall be determined according to the needs of the person entitled to receive support and the financial capacity and status of the person obligated to provide support. (Article 1120) The method of providing support shall be determined by agreement between the parties. If no agreement can be reached, it shall be determined by the family council. (Article 1121) The parties may request a change in the extent and method of support due to a change in circumstances.

Chapter 6: The Family (Article 1122) A family is a group of relatives living together for the purpose of permanent cohabitation. (Article 1123) A family has a head of the family. Persons in the same family, other than the head of the family, are all family members. A non-relative who lives in the same family for the purpose of permanent cohabitation is considered a family member. (Article 1124) The head of the family is presumed from the relatives in the family group. In the absence of such presumption, the most senior person in the family shall be the head of the family. If the seniority is the same, the oldest person shall be the head of the family. If the most senior or oldest person is unable or unwilling to manage family affairs, they shall designate a family member to act as their agent. (Article 1125) Family affairs are managed by the head of the family, but the head of the family may entrust part of the family affairs to family members for management. (Article 1126) The head of the family shall manage family affairs with attention to the interests of all family members. (Article 1127) A family member who has reached adulthood or who is married even if they have not reached adulthood may request separation from the family. (Article 1128) The head of the family may order a family member who has reached adulthood or who is married even if they have not reached adulthood to separate from the family, but only if there is a legitimate reason.

Chapter 7: The Family Council (Article 1129) When a family council should be convened according to the provisions of this law, it shall be convened by the party, legal representative, or other interested party. (Article 1130) A family council is composed of five members. (Article 1131) The members of the family council shall be determined from the following relatives of the minor, person under interdiction, or the deceased, in the following order: (1) Lineal ascendants; (2) Ascending collateral relatives within the third degree of kinship; (3) Collateral relatives of the same generation within the fourth degree of kinship. Among the persons of the same order in the preceding paragraph, the one with the closest degree of kinship shall have priority. If the degrees of kinship are the same, the relative on the paternal side shall have priority. If the system is the same and the degrees of kinship are the same, the older person shall have priority. (Article 1132) If there are no relatives as prescribed in the preceding article, or the number of relatives is insufficient to meet the legal number of members, the court may, upon application by the person with the right to convene the council, designate members from among other relatives. (Article 1133) A guardian, minor, or person under interdiction may not be a member of the family council. (Article 1134) A person who is legally required to be a member of the family council may not resign from their position without a legitimate reason. (Article 1135) A family council may not meet unless at least three members are present, and no resolution may be made without the consent of a majority of the members present. (Article 1136) A member of the family council who has a personal interest in the matter under discussion may not participate in the resolution. (Article 1137) A person with the right to convene the family council as specified in Article 1129 who is dissatisfied with the resolution of the family council may appeal to the court within three months. (End)

Local Correspondence

Suzhou 72

Further News of the Robbery in Tong'an Bridge Town. Regarding the incident in Hufang Township, Tong'an Bridge Town, where a large gang of lake bandits robbed the town around 4 PM on the 10th of this month, and kidnapped ten hostages, including Zhu Zuozhou, it was learned yesterday that after the lake bandits kidnapped the ten hostages that evening, they fled through Nanhejia Bridge, Longtang Bridge, Chenwuzhuang Bridge, and exited Taihu Lake to Xiaogong Mountain. At that time, Zhu Zuozhou, a business corps instructor who was injured during the kidnapping, died on the bandit ship due to his injuries. The bandits, considering it inauspicious, abandoned the body on the beach. The bandit ship arrived at Jinshu Port, where they interrogated the kidnapped hostages one by one regarding their family wealth. As a result, they first released Wang Jianzhong, the principal of Tong'an Elementary School, Lu Shuxun, the executive committee member of the Third District Second Branch, Chai Bingsheng, a cook from the派出所 police station, and Chen Qiao, a Jiangbei boatman. They also released a boat, which Chen Qiao sailed back to the town. The remaining hostages, Li Qianqing, the business corps minister, and merchants Jin Peizhi, Zhou Shuiquan (yesterday's report erroneously stated he was released), Zhu Shaoyu, Zhang Shunbao, and Wang Shengqiu, were not released and were taken by the bandits to the western Taihu Lake. Regarding the total losses in the town, a preliminary investigation was conducted yesterday. Fangtailong Nanhua Store estimated a loss of approximately 691.9 yuan, 321 small silver dollars, 30 角輔幣券 supplementary currency coupons, and 10,000 copper coins. Yifeng Cigarette Paper Store lost one tael and four mace of gold jewelry and 23 yuan in silver dollars. Genji Cloth Store lost 250 yuan in paper money. Donggongxing Jinghua Rice Store lost 43 yuan. Yutong Bean Cake Company lost over 40 silver dollars and 270 yuan in banknotes. Yongqingcheng Bean Cake Company lost over 100 yuan. Jendetai Nanhua Store lost 50 or 60 yuan. Qingtaiyong lost over 30 yuan. Yonglong Nanhua Store lost over 50 yuan. Zhu Gansheng's family lost 600 yuan. The loss of gold and jewelry is still under investigation. The losses of other households were minimal and are not included. Currently, the Suzhou-Wuxi land and water police forces are cooperating in the suppression efforts, but the bandits have already fled to the mountainous areas of western Taihu Lake.

Five Bandits Involved in the Tong'an Bridge Robbery Captured. The Third District Second Branch of the Public Security Bureau apprehended Yang Yuanliang, Chen Alu, Lu Aliuliu, Huang Mingrong, Lu Shi, and five other suspects involved in the Tong'an Bridge robbery at the Tianyuan Inn in Le Rong Fang outside Lümen Gate on the night before last (the 11th) at midnight, along with 90 yuan in suspected stolen silver dollars. They have been taken to the bureau for interrogation. Meanwhile, police have been dispatched to various locations to rigorously search for the remaining accomplices.

Pan Zhimao served as the Zhuang head. Every time the rent was collected, five or six people, including Fang Bohua, were hired to collect the rent rice. All the cash converted from the collected rice was deposited in the bank daily. However, there was always over a thousand yuan in cash kept in the Zhuang. The night before last (the 11th), thieves somehow broke into the Zhuang and went to the inner Zhuang room, where they opened the silver box and stole over a thousand silver dollars before escaping through the back door. It was not discovered until yesterday morning (the 13th), and the case was reported to the First Branch of the Public Security Bureau for investigation.

Qingpu 73

Several Robberies in One Week. Chen Shengcai, a fisherman from the vicinity of Dianshan River in the northeast of the Sixth District of the county, was repeatedly robbed by two bandit boats with over ten bandits on board one night last month, losing dozens of catties of crabs worth over 50 silver dollars. Three days later, in Xiyu Township, around 9 PM, four bandit boats with over thirty bandits suddenly arrived. Farmers fled at the alarm, allowing the bandits to search and rob house by house without hindrance. It is reported that over 600 yuan was stolen in total.

Township Head Arrested on Suspicion of Private Smuggling. Cheng, the township head of Shangshu Town in the Sixth District of the county, opened both a Nanhua and a meat shop in the town and has always been law-abiding. Suddenly, several police officers from the Third Branch of the Public Security Bureau were dispatched to Cheng's residence and shops to search them, claiming to be acting on a secret order from the county government, accusing Cheng of private smuggling of opium. However, after two hours of searching, nothing was found. Cheng was then taken to the bureau and sent to the county for investigation. People in the town, believing Cheng to be honest and law-abiding, feel unjustly treated and have jointly submitted a petition to the county government for his release.

Investigating the Police Extortion Case. A police officer from the First Squad of the County Police Team stationed in Zhujiajiao Town went to the Guan Di Temple in the east market of the town the night before last. Using the pretext of arresting opium smokers, he demanded 160 silver dollars from the abbot monk, Si Lan, and took pawn tickets and clothing. It is now learned that the county government has heard of this case and will rigorously investigate it.

Wuxi 74

Jiangsu Province Pawn Industry to Hold Regular Meeting. The Jiangsu Province Pawn Industry Regulations have recently been revised by the ministry and province and are scheduled to be implemented on January 1, 20 of the Republic of China. After the promulgation, the pawn industry associations of Tai, Dongtai, and Xinghua counties took the lead in pointing out that Article 16 of the newly revised regulations states, "For over five days in a month, half a month's interest is charged; for over fifteen days, one month's interest is charged." The old regulations originally stipulated that the pawn redemption month should not exceed five days. If the sixth day was exceeded, one month's interest would be charged. Now the pawn industry is extremely depressed, expenses are increasing daily, and income is declining. If the interest is reduced by half a month, pawnshops will not be able to cover their losses and will face difficulties. They jointly sent a letter to the Provincial Pawn Industry Association, requesting assistance to maintain operations. Subsequently, pawnshops in various counties responded and appealed en masse, stating that in recent years, financial resources have been exhausted and the pawn industry has plummeted. Statistics from Jiangsu Province show that nearly a hundred pawnshops have closed. This is clear evidence. Although the government has set restrictions, pawnshops seek profits to cover costs and cannot afford to lose money. It is difficult to force them. The country does not yet have public pawnshops. If pawnshops in various counties cannot survive, it will cause many poor people to lose their livelihoods, which is contrary to the government's intention to help the poor. Moreover, pawnshops in京 Shanghai and provincial capitals are not subject to the half-month interest reduction, which is particularly unfair. Therefore, over 190 pawnshops, including the pawn industry associations and offices of Tai County, Dongtai County, Xinghua County, Wujiang County, Kunshan County, Songjiang County, Dantu County, Wujin County, Yixing County, Changshu County, Liyang County, Jiangyin County, Wuxian County, and Wuxi County, have exchanged correspondence, discussing ways to cope with the situation. They decided to hold a meeting at the Wuxi County Chamber of Commerce at 2 PM on the 22nd of this month, inviting colleagues from various counties to jointly discuss rescue measures. Yesterday, they sent a notice to the pawn industry associations of various counties throughout the province, requesting them to send responsible representatives with credentials to Wuxi on time to discuss and formulate a plan.

Requesting a Flexible Account Settlement Method via Telegram. The Wuxi Chamber of Commerce has already notified all industries to comply with the national calendar for year-end account settlement and has published a notice to that effect. However, recently, it has repeatedly received letters from chambers of commerce in various counties that have dealings with Wuxi, as well as from various industries in Wuxi, stating that as winter arrives and autumn grains are harvested, various industries are in dire need of funds, and the market relies on this turnover. However, with the year-end account settlement, Shanghai is urging the closure of accounts, causing silver prices to tighten daily and the market to become depressed. Not only is commerce affected, but low grain prices harm farmers.

Moreover, the county government is busy collecting grain taxes, receiving only thirty or forty gold pieces daily, a historically low amount. If no measures are taken to provide relief, it will inevitably affect the winter grain tax collection, leading to official-civilian hardship and an unmanageable market. They have requested that the Chamber of Commerce forward their requests to the government to continue using the Jiangsu Province grain tax collection method, extending the settlement date to February 16 of the following year to rescue the market and avoid panic. The Chamber of Commerce has immediately telegraphed the National Government Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, requesting approval for a flexible approach to provide relief. It is unknown how the government will respond.

Another Bandit Involved in the Kidnapping Case Captured. Qian Tianxiong, the captain of the county police brigade's water patrol team, recently led detectives in the vicinity of Fu'an Township, Hudai Town, and captured three key suspects in the case of Feng Yunsheng, the youngest son of Yuequan, the deputy head of Shuiqiao Township, Xiaofeng Lane, Kaiyuan Township, who was kidnapped and robbed. They were sent to the brigade headquarters for interrogation. The day before yesterday afternoon, Captain Wang opened a court and interrogated them severely. One of them, Ding Asheng, 22 years old, confessed to kidnapping Feng Yuequan and demanding a huge ransom. He also revealed that there was an accomplice hiding in Outangqiao, Kaiyuan Township. Another, Zhu Shilin, and a third, Xu Baorong, both confessed that on June 4 of this year, they committed a robbery at Zhijing Nunnery in Qingshan Bay, and also shot Wang Yunyun. After Captain Wang obtained their confessions, he prepared a document yesterday and sent it to the county government for legal interrogation. Regarding the accomplice revealed by Ding Asheng, it is reported that Wang has ordered Detective Liao to cooperate with detectives to go to the countryside to arrest him, and he has already been captured.

Changshu 75

New and Old Accountants of the Finance Bureau Hand Over. Since Hao Bingzhang was transferred to任任 take over as the director of the Finance Bureau of this county, there was still a portion that had not been fully transferred from the previous director, Fei Yuhong. It was decided to hold an accounting meeting at the Finance Bureau on the afternoon of the 10th of this month. Former Director Fei sent Wu Xingwu and Gui Mengjian to Changshu in advance to represent him in the handover. On that day, Director Hao convened representatives from various party and government agencies to attend. The liquidation began at 2 PM, and the results were found to be in compliance with the listed register. However, it was noted that under the original register item, various special funds that should have been deposited with the Education Bureau, the Construction Bureau, and the District Office had all been misappropriated. Gao Tinggui, the director of the Education Bureau, denied this and requested that the funds be reclaimed, while Representative Gui stated that the funds had been used for local purposes and there were receipts for all of them. Lin Mengdan, the chief of the Finance Bureau's General Affairs Section, stated that it would not be appropriate for the new director to immediately allocate the funds. As a result, it was agreed by both parties that the 前述 a mentioned funds of over 9,000 yuan would be borrowed by former Director Fei in consultation with the new director, and that the interest would be borne by former Director Fei from the date of the loan until the date when the new director collected the tax revenues. Furthermore, Gao, Director of Education Bureau, raised the issue that the Education Bureau had not received the 6,000 yuan in surplus gun tax revenue listed in the local budget for the 18th year of the Republic of China, of which half was earmarked for education funding. Representative Gui stated that the autumn inspection last year had resulted in a reduced quality, and there was no surplus in the tax revenue collection. In the end, Deng Bingwei of the Party Department offered a conciliatory opinion that the Education Bureau's share of the tax revenue collection surplus would be subject to a further accounting after Fei, the former director, submitted a report on the income and expenditures for that item. Only then were both parties satisfied. Therefore, the handover procedure between Fei and Hao still needs to be continued.

A Firewood Boat Was Robbed in Yangcheng Lake. Qian Genfa, a resident of Dongtang City Township in this county, around 40 years old, who specialized in selling rice straw, loaded a boat with rice straw and three companions the day before yesterday and sailed to Shanghai to sell it. After mooring for two days, the straw was completely sold, yielding over 50 silver dollars. They immediately raised anchor to return to Changshu. To their surprise, while sailing in Yangcheng Lake at around 11 PM, two small boats suddenly sped out of the reeds and approached their boat. Suddenly, over ten bandits wielding sharp blades and wooden sticks jumped onto Qian's boat, ordering them to stop. They first bound Qian Genfa and his boat companions with麻 hemp rope and placed them in the stern cabin. Then, they rampaged through the boat, searching and robbing. As a result, they robbed over 50 silver dollars from the sale, as well as two bolts of factory cloth and one umbrella that fellow villagers had entrusted Qian to purchase. Before leaving, they also injured Qian with a stick.

The County Government Re-examines the Strange Youth. A strange youth was discovered in the vicinity of Haitang Sanlidao outside Dadongmen in this county last month. He panicked and said that bandit troops were retreating from Kunshan and were passing through Changshu to cross the river, and he called for shops to close and stopped pedestrians from passing. Zhou Zhongshan, a merchant, reported the incident to the Dong District Business Corps, who detained the youth and sent him to the Public Security Bureau, which in turn sent him to the county judiciary for interrogation. Yesterday (the 10th) afternoon, the county government specially summoned witnesses Zhou Zhongshan and Jin Shengding, as well as Wu Kunyuan, a member of the Business Corps, and the defendant Zhou Bingxing, among others. Shen, the审员 judicial officer, opened a court for re-examination. According to Zhou Bingxing's testimony, "That night, I was drunk and confused for a moment. I was fooled by Feng Alin. I came to know Feng because I delivered soup to him. That day, Feng said to me, 'I'll ask you to do something, and it will only take two hours, and I'll give you two silver dollars.' Because I wanted silver dollars, I agreed to do it. Now I don't know where Feng is. In short, I was fooled by someone and I ask for forgiveness." Subsequently, because further investigation was still needed, the county government ordered Zhou Bingxing to be remanded in custody.

The Yong'an Steamboat Was Robbed by Bandits. The Feiyun steamship of the Wuyi Yong'an Steamship Bureau, which was sailing to Zangcun, Yixing, departed from Changzhou with passengers at noon on the 10th. As it approached Zhanghe Bridge, it was already dusk. Suddenly, five or six bandits on the shore fired guns at the driver, preventing the ship from continuing. At the same time, a bandit ship in the river came head-on in front of the steamship, firing shots in response. The steamship had no choice but to stop. The bandits then rushed onto the ship, first robbing the passengers of their silver dollars, then rummaging through boxes and chests in the accounting room, emptying it completely. At this time, the bandits saw three injured people in the cabin, lying down and moaning. They forced the steamship to tow their boat to Zhangshiqiao in West Taihu Lake, before allowing it to return. Mei Changgen and Ms. Shen's injuries were the most serious. News this morning (the 12th) reported that Ms. Shen had died in the hospital due to her injuries.

Liaoning····Temporarily Continue to Follow the Old Holiday Schedule

Anhui····Only One Day of Holiday for the New Year

Liaoning Shenyang News: The Liaoning Education Department, having previously received an order from the Ministry of Education that schools should not continue to take the old lunar New Year holiday and that the winter vacation should be changed to three weeks during the national calendar New Year in order to promote the national calendar, deliberated and decided that, due to budgetary reasons in the province, it would continue to take the winter vacation as usual. The holiday period was set for forty days, from January 14 to February 22. The national calendar New Year holiday would be three days. However, in order to promote the national calendar, all lunar New Year entertainment activities would be changed to be held around the national calendar New Year. It would then submit a request for changes during next year's winter vacation and summer vacation.

Anhui: The Anhui Education Department Secretariat sent a letter to all schools yesterday changing the dates of the winter vacation. The letter read as follows: "Recently, the principals of various schools came to the department and stated that if the national calendar New Year holiday dates stipulated by the Ministry were implemented, many difficulties would arise. Please approve a change." After review, this was found to be true. Apart from January 1 of the 20th year of the Republic of China, which will be a holiday, it is temporarily approved to take a four-week consecutive holiday starting from January 26. After the holiday period, classes should resume as usual without delay. In addition to separate letters, the above is hereby conveyed for your information. December 6.

Local News

Elementary School Party Doctrine Speech Contest 89

—Tomorrow the final will be held at the City Chamber of Commerce—

See Who Among the Eighteen Contestants Will Take First Place

The Third Group Preliminary Competition Concluded Yesterday

The Shanghai City Party Headquarters Training Department's city-wide elementary school student Party doctrine speech contest, has been holding preliminary rounds in groups for several days, and the situation is very lively. Yesterday was the date for the third group preliminary competition. At 1 p.m., it was still held in the City Party Headquarters Auditorium. More than 300 contestants and audience members from 20 schools attended. The students' speeches were also quite wonderful. As a result, six students were selected (because the scores for fifth and sixth place were the same). So far, the preliminary competition has come to an end. It is scheduled to hold the final at the T'ien Hau Temple Bridge City Chamber of Commerce at 1 p.m. tomorrow to determine the final winners. Moreover, the number of places taken yesterday and today were both six. The first group also took five places, so the Pudong Attached Elementary School, which had a score one point lower than the fifth place, was selected. Therefore, a total of eighteen students were selected from the preliminary rounds of each group to participate in tomorrow's final. During the final, each school must select students from all grades (at least twenty students) to attend the lecture for observation and learning. The results of yesterday's third group are recorded below: First (De Run) Zuo Yongbao, Second (First Experimental Elementary School) Jiang Meiyun, Third (Zhen Ru) Yang Shiqi, Fourth (Wan Zhu) Liao Zhijun, Fifth (Xi Cheng) Yuan Baoyue (Hai Shan) Shen Ruibin.

National Chi Nan University College of Education Invites Cheng Shixu to Give a Lecture 91

The College of Education of National Chi Nan University invited Cheng Shixu, Director of the Fujian Department of Education, to give a lecture at the school yesterday at 3 p.m. President Xie Xunchu gave an introductory speech. About 300 people attended the lecture. Cheng spoke about his hopes for the College of Education. A: How to cultivate true educators must focus on practical investigation and verification. He also cited Dr. Paul Monroe's visit to China, saying that although the doctor is old, he is still so enthusiastic and does not hesitate to travel far. He is conducting a detailed investigation of the current political, educational, and social conditions in China before defining education and fulfilling his responsibilities. Since the National Chi Nan University College of Education is responsible for the mission of overseas Chinese education, observation of overseas Chinese education is essential. B: The College of Education should cultivate an excellent school spirit: (1) Personality influence, (2) Scholarly life, (3) Educator's aspirations. He explained it in great detail and his words were very sincere. He also spoke of the cultivation he gained during his prison life, which was humorous and moving.

Qiangshu Vocational Middle School in Shanghai County Preparing for Horticultural Lecture Conference 94

Lecture Period: From the 24th of this Month to January 3rd of the 20th Year

Lecturers include Niu Yongjian, Gao Yang, and 14 Others

Limited to 60 Attendees, Registration Begins Immediately

Niu Yongjian, a member of the school affairs committee of Qiangshu Vocational Middle School in the Sixth District of Shanghai County, and others, in order to promote horticulture, improve the appearance of villages and fields, and develop the rural economy, are taking advantage of the New Year holiday to jointly organize a horticultural lecture conference with the Sixth District Office's Yu Tang Public Education Center. Qualifications for attendees: A. Teachers and staff of all levels of schools in the county. B. Local autonomous government officials. C. Those who are interested in studying rural affairs. Lecture period: From December 24th of the 19th year to January 3rd of the 20th year, two hours each in the morning and afternoon every day. Those who wish to attend must register with the association before the 18th of this month. Those in remote areas can register by mail. Attendance is limited to 60 people. If attendees from various places meet qualifications A and B, they may be reimbursed for travel expenses as appropriate. The conference address is Qiangshu Vocational Middle School, Maqiao Town, Sixth District, Shanghai. Lecture subjects include: General knowledge of horticulture, Essentials of landscape architecture, Essentials of seedling cultivation, Cooperation between landscape architecture and the farmers' economy and rural organization, Essentials of fruit tree cultivation, Landscape architecture and rural improvement, Horticulture, raising chickens and bees, and other topics. The lecturers who have been hired include Shen Daonan, a horticultural expert who studied in France; Shen Qinghui, a technician at the Shanghai County Farm; Li Chuan, director of horticulture at Qiangshu Vocational Middle School; Zhou Shili, a horticultural expert who studied in France and a professor at the National Labor University; Guo Xujing, a horticultural expert who studied in France and director of the College of Agriculture at National Central University; Gao Yang, President of Jiangsu Provincial College of Education and Director of the Yu Tang Public Education Center; Lu Feizhi, a horticultural expert who studied in the United States and Chief of the First Section of the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Agriculture and Mining; Xu Keming and Zhang Yu, horticultural experts; Zan Xian, special cooperation instructor from the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Agriculture and Mining; Ku Jianan, an agricultural expert who studied in France and President of Jiangsu Agricultural College; and Niu Yongjian and Niu Changyao, members of the school affairs committee of Qiangshu Vocational Middle School, and Principal Huai Ren, and more than ten other people. The association will provide board and lodging for the attendees. All expenses are donated by Mr. Niu Yongjian, it is said.

Arima Cup China-Japan International Table Tennis Tournament 110

Held at 8:00 PM Tonight

The Arima Earl Cup China-Japan International Table Tennis Tournament will be held at 8:00 PM tonight on the fifth floor of the Daily News Agency at Shenjiawan Road, Wusong Road. All arrangements have been agreed upon by Yu Binqi and Zou Guxin, the presidents of the Shanghai Table Tennis Federation, and the Japanese team's Mr. Manabe and Mr. Ikeda. The general arrangements are as follows: The first tournament will be hosted by the Japanese team, and the second tournament will be hosted by the Chinese team, alternating in turn. Each team will be responsible for its own profits and losses. There were serious negotiations regarding the use of balls, and it was decided that when the tournament is hosted by the Japanese team, PA balls will be used, and when it is hosted by the Chinese team, Chain Brand balls produced by the China Table Tennis Company will be used. The Japanese team also agreed to use Chinese balls in the future. The above matters will be approved at the staff meeting tonight. The players and staff attending tonight are: Referee Zhang Yongchu, Yu Binqi (referee and representative of the Federation), Zou Guxin (team leader), Yang Xiqing and Wang Mengnian (recorders), and Lu Xiulu.

Players: Lu Shenqiu, Lu Tong, Zhou Jianwen, Luo Hongsheng, Huang Xiangfa, Lu Hanjun, Zhou Weixin, Wu Manqing (reserve), Chuan Jiyi, Chen Zhaowen. Tickets are two jiao each and can be purchased at the Chinese Typewriter Company at the intersection of Nanjing Road and Jiangxi Road, Yu Binqi, and at the Koga Store on Wusong Road. In addition, the Shanghai Table Tennis Federation has consulted with the China Table Tennis Company regarding the national significance of this event, and the company has donated a beautiful outfit to the team to boost their morale. The China Company's generosity and assistance are deeply appreciated, it is said.

Report on Yesterday's Xiqing Basketball Games 115

Zhenru Beats Zhonggong (A) 40 to 33

Chizhi Beats Jiangwan (A) 39 to 15

Yuezhong Beats Youai (B) 25 to 15

Three Xiqing basketball games were held last night starting at 7:00 PM. The results were (1) In Group A, Zhenru beat Zhonggong 40 to 33, (2) In Group A, Chizhi beat Jiangwan 19 to 15, (3) In Group B, Yuezhong beat Youai 25 to 15.

(1) Zhenru Beats Zhonggong (A) Zhenru played with the force of thousands of troops and horses, causing Zhonggong to fall apart. In the first half, Zhenru scored 27 points, and Zhonggong scored 8 points. In the second half, Zhenru was tired and its lineup was disrupted. Zhonggong then surged forward like a tide and invaded in a big way. The closest the score came was 38 to 33. In the end, Zhenru won 40 to 33.

Chizhi committed 14 fouls, and Jiangwan committed 9 fouls. In the end, Chizhi scored 39 points, and Jiangwan scored 15 points.

Local News

Opposition to Water Rate Increase 118

Taxpayers' Association Resolves on Countermeasures

Real Estate Association to Convene Meeting Today

The Public Concession's water rate increase case, ever since the company adopted high-pressure tactics by cutting off water to Zhang Tiankai, a resident of Connaught Road, and the Hua Shang villas on Peng Road, has aroused serious public attention. The Taxpayers' Association is also actively engaged in negotiations. The details heard yesterday are recorded below:

The Chinese Taxpayers' Association convened a meeting of its Standing Committee at noon yesterday. Present were Chairman Wang Xiaolai, Vice Chairman Xu Jilong, Standing Committee members Lu Feibohong and Hu Fengxiang, Chinese Directors Yu Qiaqing, Yuan Ludeng, Xu Xinliu, and Liu Hongsheng, Chinese Committee members Qian Longzhang and Wu Yunzhai, and Secretaries Yan Esheng, Tao Leqin, and He Haikui. First, the secretaries reported on the water cut-off situation in various areas. Next, Yu Qiaqing reported. After detailed discussion by all attendees, it was unanimously agreed that the matter concerned the life and safety of residents of the Public Concession and should be handled with utmost seriousness. All countermeasures decided upon were assigned to the attendees for their respective responsibilities. Details will not be disclosed for the time being. The important points are: (1) the Public Works Department should be requested to adopt public opinion and revise the contract; (2) the water company must restore water supply and must not engage in such oppressive actions again in the future.

The Shanghai Real Estate Association, upon receiving reports of the water company's water cut-off, immediately held a meeting of responsible personnel and decided not to succumb to such high-pressure tactics. It was decided to convene an emergency meeting today (the 13th) at 4 p.m. to discuss countermeasures, and telegrams were sent out for appeal. The telegrams are recorded separately below: (To the British Government) To the British Consul-General in Shanghai, the British Minister in Peiping, and the British Cabinet and Parliament in London: The Shanghai Waterworks Company, a British enterprise, coerced residents to increase water rates and cut off water supply yesterday, engaging in a throat-grabbing blackmail. The lives of millions of residents are in imminent danger. Public sentiment is indignant, and the situation is serious. We specially request that you immediately order the restoration of the original state and the continued water supply to uphold humanitarianism and maintain Sino-British amity. Shanghai Real Estate Association, December 12. (Submitted to Government Authorities) To the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the Ministry of the Interior, and the Shanghai Municipal Government in Nanjing: The British-owned Shanghai Waterworks Company, failing to coerce a rate increase, cut off water supply yesterday, endangering the lives of millions of residents. We urgently telegraph to request intervention to restore water supply. Awaiting your orders. Shanghai Real Estate Association bows. (Notice to All Members) Sirs: Because the British-owned Shanghai Waterworks Company has failed to increase rates and disregarded the survival rights of residents, the specific principles of public utilities, and the provisions of criminal law, it cut off water supply the day before yesterday. The lives and property of millions of residents are endangered. We have specifically decided to convene an emergency meeting at 4 p.m. on December 13 (Saturday). We hereby write to request your attendance at that time. If you send a representative, please grant them full authority.

The Attitude of the Public Works Department: Yesterday, our reporter interviewed Mr. Jones of the Public Works Department regarding the water rate increase issue. According to his reply, in October, due to the high price of gold and low price of silver, the Board of Directors had no choice but to approve the water company's rate increase. At that time, there were five Chinese directors as their representatives participating in the meeting. When the Public Works Department discussed the case, it also took into account the interests of all citizens and conducted a very precise and detailed study. There are two standards for water charges: one is calculated according to the water meter, and the other is calculated according to the house rent. Currently, the Shanghai Waterworks Company calculates according to house rent. This system is beneficial to residents of the middle and lower classes and unfavorable to the upper class. Because if the amount of water used is the same, the upper-class residents pay more, and the middle and lower-class residents pay less. For example, if we take three classes of residents, upper, middle, and lower, each with a family of five, each person uses 33 gallons of water per month, and the whole family uses 165 gallons. Assuming a charge of 6% of the house rent, those with a house rent of 10 yuan pay 6 jiao per month, those with a house rent of 50 yuan pay 3 yuan per month, those with a house rent of 100 taels pay 6 taels per month, and those with a house rent of 200 taels pay 12 taels per month. Using the same amount of water, one pays 12 taels and the other pays 6 jiao. The water fees paid by upper-class residents exceed the cost of water, while the water fees paid by middle and lower-class residents are less. In order to take care of the interests of the majority of people and the water company, the Public Works Department had to take from the rich to make up for the poor. If calculated by water meter, the water fees paid by upper, middle, and lower-class citizens would be equal. The result would be an average increase of 20% in water fees, which would increase the burden on middle and lower-class citizens even more. The water company is very happy to convert the city to water meters. However, it would cost two to three million yuan and take two to three years to complete. Furthermore, according to Mr. Pearson, the General Engineer and Manager of the Waterworks Company, the company plans to convene a shareholders' meeting to discuss the issue of changing to water meters. The Public Works Department has also agreed in principle, believing this is the only way to open the current difficulty and the only way to restrain citizens' water use. As for the company having cut off water supply, it is only to two families because they owe three months of water fees. There are also many families who have paid the increased rates. This statement is somewhat biased towards the company's side. However, in order to study the truth of the matter, we must collect the opinions of all parties and make a fair judgment. Therefore, we present them together.

Xiong Shihui, Yang Yongtai

Funeral Held for Zeng Chunfan Yesterday Morning

Wang Boqun to Arrive in Shanghai Soon

Regarding the crash of the China National Aviation Corporation's Shanghai aircraft, the funeral for Xiong Shihui's severely injured and deceased bodyguard, Zeng Chunfan, was held yesterday morning, and the coffin was temporarily placed in the Zheshao Guild Hall. Dr. Niu, along with doctors Zeng Baohan and Chen Jiayu, changed the dressing on the wound. There was no change in the wound. He urinated spontaneously twice. Temperature was 99.4 degrees Fahrenheit at 2:00 p.m., pulse 92, respiration 20. He was in very good spirit and constantly asked questions when seeing the doctor. The cough was slightly better.
